org.apache.kafka.connect.runtime.isolation package. The system comprises three main components:\\n\\n1. **Custom ClassLoader Hierarchy**:\\n   - PluginClassLoader (extends URLClassLoader): A child-first classloader that loads plugin classes in isolation from a specified location. Implemented in connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginClassLoader.java.\\n   - DelegatingClassLoader (extends URLClassLoader): Acts as the parent that delegates to individual PluginClassLoaders using a child-first delegation model. Implemented in connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/DelegatingClassLoader.java.\\n   - ClassLoaderFactory: Factory for creating PluginClassLoader and DelegatingClassLoader instances, located in connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ClassLoaderFactory.java.\\n\\n2. **Plugin Discovery and Reflection-based Scanning**:\\n   - PluginScanner (abstract base class): Defines the plugin discovery strategy with implementations for both reflective scanning and service loading. Located in connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginScanner.java.\\n   - ReflectionScanner: Uses ClassGraph library to scan for plugin implementations via reflection, discovering classes that implement/extend the plugin interfaces (Converter, HeaderConverter, SourceConnector, SinkConnector, etc.). Implemented in connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ReflectionScanner.java.\\n   - ServiceLoaderScanner: Uses Java ServiceLoader mechanism to discover plugins from META-INF/services files. Implemented in connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ServiceLoaderScanner.java.\\n   - PluginDiscoveryMode (enum): Controls whether to use only ServiceLoader, only reflection, or hybrid modes with/without warnings. Implemented in connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginDiscoveryMode.java.\\n\\n3. **Interface-based Dependency Injection for Plugin Types**:\\n   - Converter interface: Defines the contract for data converters in connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/Converter.java. Implementations use the config() method to provide ConfigDef for dependency injection.\\n   - HeaderConverter interface: Specifically for header conversion in connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/HeaderConverter.java, with config() for dependency injection.\\n   - Connector (abstract base class): Root interface for all connectors in connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/connector/Connector.java, defining version(), config(), and other required methods.\\n   - SourceConnector: Extends Connector for source connectors in connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/source/SourceConnector.java.\\n   - SinkConnector: Extends Connector for sink connectors in connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/sink/SinkConnector.java.\\n\\n4. **Supporting Infrastructure**:\\n   - Plugins (main orchestrator): The primary class that manages plugin discovery, instantiation, and dependency injection. Implements newPlugin(), newConverter(), newHeaderConverter(), and newConnector() methods. Located in connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/Plugins.java.\\n   - PluginDesc: Descriptor for discovered plugins containing class, version, and location information. Located in connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginDesc.java.\\n   - PluginScanResult: Aggregates all discovered plugins by type. Located in connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginScanResult.java.\\n   - PluginSource: Represents a plugin source (classpath or isolated jar) with its type and URLs. Located in connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginSource.java.\\n   - PluginType (enum): Enumerates all plugin types (SOURCE, SINK, CONVERTER, HEADER_CONVERTER, TRANSFORMATION, PREDICATE, CONFIGPROVIDER, REST_EXTENSION, CONNECTOR_CLIENT_CONFIG_OVERRIDE_POLICY). Located in connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginType.java.\\n   - PluginUtils: Utility methods for plugin discovery, version matching, alias generation, and source creation. Located in connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginUtils.java.\\n   - LoaderSwap: Helper for switching classloaders in try-with-resources statements. Located in connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/LoaderSwap.java.\\n   - VersionedPluginLoadingException: Exception for plugin loading errors with version information. Located in connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/VersionedPluginLoadingException.java.\\n   - AbstractHerder: Orchestrates plugin loading and dependency injection at the worker level. Located in connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/AbstractHerder.java.\\n   - Worker: Creates plugin instances and manages their lifecycle. Located in connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/Worker.java.\\n\\nThe system implements a sophisticated pattern where: (1) Plugins are discovered through reflection or service loading, (2) Each plugin type is assigned to an isolated or classpath classloader, (3) Plugin instantiation occurs through dependency injection by discovering ConfigDef specifications, (4) Multiple versions of plugins can coexist, resolved via version ranges, and (5) All communication with plugins occurs through standardized interfaces to maintain loose coupling and enable versioning.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":11,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1329,"cache_read_input_tokens":91839,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1329},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"ac747317-d8ab-4d2f-9990-71e71c48e03f","uuid":"5d6eace3-4ea8-4fcb-95e6-43c52062e6d8"}

Implemented in connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ReflectionScanner.java.\\n   - ServiceLoaderScanner: Uses Java ServiceLoader mechanism to discover plugins from META-INF/services files. Implemented in connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ServiceLoaderScanner.java.\\n   - PluginDiscoveryMode (enum): Controls whether to use only ServiceLoader, only reflection, or hybrid modes with/without warnings. Implemented in connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginDiscoveryMode.java.\\n\\n3. **Interface-based Dependency Injection for Plugin Types**:\\n   - Converter interface: Defines the contract for data converters in connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/Converter.java. Implementations use the config() method to provide ConfigDef for dependency injection.\\n   - HeaderConverter interface: Specifically for header conversion in connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/HeaderConverter.java, with config() for dependency injection.\\n   - Connector (abstract base class): Root interface for all connectors in connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/connector/Connector.java, defining version(), config(), and other required methods.\\n   - SourceConnector: Extends Connector for source connectors in connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/source/SourceConnector.java.\\n   - SinkConnector: Extends Connector for sink connectors in connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/sink/SinkConnector.java.\\n\\n4. **Supporting Infrastructure**:\\n   - Plugins (main orchestrator): The primary class that manages plugin discovery, instantiation, and dependency injection. Located in connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginUtils.java.\\n   - LoaderSwap: Helper for switching classloaders in try-with-resources statements. Located in connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/VersionedPluginLoadingException.java.\\n   - AbstractHerder: Orchestrates plugin loading and dependency injection at the worker level. Located in connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/AbstractHerder.java.\\n   - Worker: Creates plugin instances and manages their lifecycle. Located in connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/Worker.java.\\n\\nThe system implements a sophisticated pattern where: (1) Plugins are discovered through reflection or service loading, (2) Each plugin type is assigned to an isolated or classpath classloader, (3) Plugin instantiation occurs through dependency injection by discovering ConfigDef specifications, (4) Multiple versions of plugins can coexist, resolved via version ranges, and (5) All communication with plugins occurs through standardized interfaces to maintain loose coupling and enable versioning.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
